!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究解决了单晶金刚石薄膜难以大规模集成到纳米光子量子系统中的制造问题，通过开发一种半导体兼容的直接键合工艺，成功将超薄金刚石薄膜并行键合到硅晶圆上，实现了创纪录的剪切强度，为高性能量子技术平台提供了可扩展的制造路线。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 本研究实现了基于单晶金刚石独特材料特性的纳米光子量子系统的制造。我们通过引入一种半导体兼容工艺，将多个高质量超薄金刚石薄膜直接键合至承载晶圆，从而实现了后续光电集成电路的并行纳米加工。该技术的核心是一种新型金刚石表面处理方法，该方法避免了沸腾三酸混合物的使用，同时制备出异常洁净的20微米厚单晶薄片。这些薄片被并排键合至100毫米二氧化硅晶圆上，其（100）取向金刚石键合界面实现了45.1 MPa的创纪录剪切强度，超越了所有已报道的键合尝试。证据表明该键合主要由范德华相互作用主导，这很可能源于Si-OH与C-OH表面终端之间不匹配的质子化机制，而非共价键驱动机制。尽管具有这种非分子特性，异质结构在液体浸没和标准纳米加工步骤中仍保持稳定。由于该方法主要依赖于表面洁净度与粗糙度而非特定化学反应，因此可广泛适用于各类晶圆材料。这种将超薄单晶金刚石薄膜并行键合至大面积衬底的能力，为纳米光子量子技术、高功率电子器件、微机电系统及生物技术等领域的高性能平台提供了可扩展的制备路径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> This work unlocks the manufacturing of nanophotonic quantum systems that exploit the unique material properties of single-crystal diamond (SCD). We achieve this by introducing a semiconductor-compatible process for the direct bonding of multiple high-quality, ultrathin diamond films onto a carrier wafer, enabling the subsequent parallel nanofabrication of optoelectronic integrated circuits. Central to this approach is a new diamond surface-preparation method that avoids boiling tri-acid mixtures while producing exceptionally clean 20 um thin single crystals. These platelets are bonded side-by-side to 100 mm silica wafers and exhibit a record shear strength of 45.1 MPa for (100)-oriented diamond, surpassing all previously reported bonding attempts. Evidence indicates that the bonding is dominated by van der Waals interactions, likely arising from mismatched protonation mechanisms between Si-OH and C-OH surface terminations, rather than from covalent-bond-driven mechanisms. Despite this non-molecular nature, the heterostructures remain stable through liquid immersions and standard nanofabrication steps. Because the method depends primarily on surface cleanliness and roughness rather than specific chemistries, it is broadly transferable across wafer materials. This capability to parallel-bond ultrathin SCD films onto large-area substrates provides a scalable route to high-performance platforms spanning nanophotonic quantum technologies, high-power electronics, MEMS, and biotechnology.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: single-crystal diamond, direct bonding, quantum optoelectronics, nanophotonic quantum systems, wafer-scale integration, van der Waals interactions, scalable manufacturing, heterostructure stability

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们展示了一种新型磁光阱（MOT）构型，该构型采用一对简单的交叉导线（旋转45度）配合适当的偏置场，实现了原子数超过10^8的磁光阱。随后，通过微调控制参数，利用同一对导线对原子进行磁囚禁，并通过强制蒸发冷却将其冷却为原子数超过10^4的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate, BEC）。
> 
> 我们提出了使用任意旋转角度交叉导线对产生四极磁场的理论框架，并介绍了原子芯片的设计与制备工艺。最后，我们描述了仅使用单一交叉导线原子芯片实现玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体制备所需的实验方案。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We demonstrate a new magneto-optical trap (MOT) configuration using a simple pair of crossed wires rotated at 45 deg and an appropriate bias field to generate a MOT of >10^8 atoms. The same pair of wires, with slightly adjusted control parameters, is then used to magnetically trap the atoms and cool them via forced evaporative cooling into a Bose-Einstein condensate (BEC) with >10^4 atoms.
>   We present the theoretical framework for generating a quadrupole field using a pair of crossed wires with arbitrary rotation angle, along with the atom chip design and fabrication. Finally, we describe the experimental protocols required for BEC production using only a single crossed-wire atom chip.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: magneto-optical trap, Bose-Einstein condensate, crossed wires, atom chip, evaporative cooling, quadrupole field, experimental protocol

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了在集成光学电路中利用经典和非经典态进行量子储层计算，发现仅使用单一量子输入模式即可显著降低分类错误率，为高效量子计算提供了新方向。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子储备计算是一种对硬件实现友好的量子神经网络方案，其物理系统需求极低，且已被证明相较于经典方案具有优势。我们采用扩展的正-P相空间方法，高效模拟了一种基于线性硅芯片的玻色子量子储备计算系统，该系统由单一非经典态——“小猫态”激发。结合输入编码的相干态，我们的方法能够在无需希尔伯特空间截断的情况下，精确获取所有关联函数。令人惊讶的是，我们发现仅凭单个输入模式所提供的“量子性”，便足以在分类误差上实现相较于经典方案显著（超过9倍）的降低。我们的研究为利用易得的光学硬件实现高效量子计算提供了一个前景广阔的方向。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum reservoir computing (QRC) is a hardware-implementation-friendly quantum neural network scheme with minimal physical system requirements and a proven advantage over classical counterparts. We use an extension of the positive-P phase space method to efficiently simulate a bosonic, linear silicon-chip based QRC system excited with a single nonclassical state, a "kitten" state. In combination with input-encoding coherent states, our method allows to obtain exact results for all correlation functions without Hilbert space cutoff. Surprisingly, we find that such a setting - where the only "quantumness'' derives from a single input mode, is sufficient to obtain significant (over 9-fold) reduction of classification error over the classical counterpart. Our work provides a promising direction toward efficient quantum computation with accessible optical hardware.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum reservoir computing, integrated optical circuit, classical states, nonclassical states, silicon-chip, positive-P phase space, classification error reduction, quantum computation

### 255. ❌ A quadratic Grassmann manifold optimization problem arising from quantum embedding methods

**作者**: Thomas Ayral, Eric Cancès, Fabian M. Faulstich, Lin Lin, Alicia Negre
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

**评分理由**: 论文标题和摘要明确表明这是一篇纯数学和计算物理领域的论文，研究Grassmann流形上的二次优化问题及其在量子嵌入方法中的应用。全文未提及任何医学图像分析、深度学习、疾病诊断、手术规划或医疗AI相关内容。所有关键词均与医学图像分析领域相关，而论文主题是数学优化和量子化学计算，两者领域完全不同，因此所有关键词相关度均为0。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    本文研究了Grassmann流形上的二次优化问题，提出了通过求解辅助凸问题获得全局最小值或改进优化算法初始化的方法，该研究源于量子嵌入方法中浴轨道构造的应用。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 本文针对格拉斯曼流形 ${\rm Gr}(m,\mathbb R^M)$ 上最小化二次函数 $J(P) = \text{Tr}(BP)- \frac{1}{2} \text{Tr}(A P A P)$ 的优化问题（其中 $A,B \in \mathbb R^{M \times M}_{\rm sym}$，且 $A \succeq 0$）提出了数学分析和数值求解策略。尽管该问题是非凸的，通常存在非全局的局部极小值——这对黎曼优化和自洽场（Self-Consistent Field, SCF）算法构成了挑战——但我们识别出了一类情形，其全局极小值可以通过求解一个辅助凸问题获得。当此方法无法直接应用时，辅助问题的解仍可为黎曼优化方法和SCF算法提供有效的初始化，从而显著提升其性能。本研究的动机源于量子嵌入方法中的应用，特别是在构建浴轨道（bath orbitals）时，此类优化问题会自然出现。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> This article presents a mathematical analysis and numerical strategies for solving the optimization problem of minimizing the quadratic function $J(P) = \text{Tr}(BP)- \frac{1}{2} \text{Tr}(A P A P)$, where $A,B \in \mathbb R^{M \times M}_{\rm sym}$, with $A \succeq 0$, over the Grassmann manifold ${\rm Gr}(m,\mathbb R^M)$. While this problem is non-convex and typically admits non-global local minima - posing challenges for Riemannian optimization and self-consistent field (SCF) algorithms - we identify cases where the global minimizer can be obtained by solving an auxiliary convex problem. When this approach is not directly applicable, the solution to the auxiliary problem still serves as an effective initialization for Riemannian optimization methods and SCF algorithms, significantly improving their performance. This work is motivated by applications in quantum embedding methods, particularly in the construction of bath orbitals, where such optimization problems naturally arise.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Grassmann manifold, quadratic optimization, Riemannian optimization, quantum embedding methods, bath orbitals, self-consistent field algorithms, convex optimization, non-convex optimization

### 256. ❌ Quantifying entanglement in quantum thermodynamics via separability constraints

**作者**: Joan Alba, Laura Ares, Jan Sperling, Julien Pinske
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17

<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子热力学中的纠缠问题，通过可分离态约束量化纠缠对热力学效应的影响，应用于量子电池和量子制冷机等系统。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析和临床AI应用，而论文完全不涉及医学、影像、诊断、手术或任何医疗相关内容，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过约束量子系统为非纠缠态来量化纠缠对热力学中热和工作的贡献，解决了纠缠在热力学中作用的问题，并应用于量子电池和制冷机等系统。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子纠缠在热力学系统中的作用仍不明确。纠缠究竟会带来热力学优势，还是构成根本性限制？本文中，我们明确量化了量子系统中因纠缠存在而产生的热量与功。这是通过将系统的非平衡动力学约束在可分离态上实现的，从而分离出纠缠对热力学效应的影响。与仅表明纠缠与热力学性质存在松散关联的热力学纠缠度量不同，施加约束构成对系统的主动干预——这回答了系统的热力学行为在多大程度上是由其量子性所导致（而非仅仅相关）。我们通过将约束动力学应用于多个多体系统（包括量子电池与量子制冷机）对本理论进行了基准验证。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The role of quantum entanglement in thermodynamical systems remains elusive. Does entanglement result in thermodynamic advantages or does it impose fundamental limitations? Here, we unambiguously quantify the amount of heat and work in a quantum system that is due to the presence of entanglement. This is achieved by constraining the system's non-equilibrium dynamics to separable states, thereby isolating the impact entanglement has on thermodynamic effects. Unlike thermodynamic entanglement measures, which signify a loose connection between entanglement and thermodynamic properties, imposing a constraint constitutes an active intervention into a system -- answering how much of a system's thermodynamics is caused by (not correlated with) its quantumness. We benchmark our theory by applying the constrained dynamics to several multipartite systems, including quantum batteries and quantum refrigerators.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum entanglement, thermodynamics, separability constraints, quantum batteries, quantum refrigerators, heat and work quantification, non-equilibrium dynamics, multipartite systems

### 257. ❌ Generation of many-body Bell correlations with short-range interactions in analog and digital quantum simulators

**作者**: Marcin Płodzień, Jan Chwedeńczuk
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17071v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17071v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子模拟器中的量子关联生成，属于量子物理和量子计算领域，与医学图像分析、人工智能临床决策支持等医学领域完全无关。所有关键词均涉及医学应用，而论文未提及任何医学相关内容，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了在具有短程相互作用的模拟和数字量子模拟器中，如何通过自旋链模型有效生成多体贝尔关联和自旋压缩态，用于量子计量和违反贝尔不等式。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子资源（如多体纠缠或贝尔关联）的动态生成可通过单轴扭曲动力学实现，该过程要求全耦合相互作用。然而，当前数字与模拟量子仿真平台原生提供的是短程或幂律耦合，其衰减过快而无法直接满足此需求。本文证明，两种自旋-$\tfrac12$链模型——交错最近邻XXX链与长程XXZ链——在投影至对称子空间时会产生等效的单轴扭曲非线性。研究表明，这些动力学可生成具有计量实用价值的自旋压缩态以及格林伯格-霍恩-塞林格相干性，从而保证多体贝尔不等式的违背。通过与精确动力学对比，我们验证了该映射的准确性，并证明所生成的关联可通过单个探测量子比特进行读取。由此产生的动力学可利用模拟与数字量子仿真器实现。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The dynamical generation of quantum resources, such as many-body entanglement or Bell correlations, can be achieved via one-axis twisting (OAT) dynamics, which require all-to-all couplings. However, current digital and analog quantum simulation platforms natively provide short-range or power-law couplings that decay too quickly for this purpose. We demonstrate that two spin-$\tfrac12$ chain models -- a staggered nearest-neighbor XXX chain and a long-range XXZ chain -- develop an effective OAT nonlinearity when projected onto the symmetric sector. We show that these dynamics generate metrologically useful spin-squeezed states and Greenberger-Horne-Zeilinger coherences that ensure violation of many-body Bell inequalities. We confirm the accuracy of this mapping by comparing it to the exact dynamics and demonstrate that the generated correlations can be read out using a single probe qubit. The resulting dynamics can be simulated with analog and digital quantum simulators

</details>
<br>

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是量子计算中时间依赖哈密顿量的全量子变分动力学模拟方法，属于量子计算和量子化学领域。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析、人工智能医疗应用等医学领域，与论文的量子计算核心内容完全无关。论文未涉及任何医学影像、疾病诊断、手术规划或医疗AI模型相关内容。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种用于模拟时间依赖哈密顿量动力学的全量子算法，通过Chebyshev谱离散化和量子奇异值变换，避免了经典反馈并实现了指数收敛，为时间依赖量子模拟提供了系统性的全量子解决方案。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 目前通过量子计算模拟含时哈密顿量动力学最广泛的方法依赖于量子-经典混合变分量子时间演化算法，其中通过经典模拟结合时间离散化方法求解决定时间演化的变分系数常微分方程组。本文提出一种全量子方法：通过切比雪夫谱离散化方法将变分系数的常微分方程组转化为静态线性方程组，并借助量子奇异值变换算法进行求解。我们的全量子算法避免了经典反馈回路，对光滑哈密顿量可实现指数级收敛，且生成的量子电路深度与时间步数无关。我们展示了两种实现策略——面向容错架构设计的全局形式，以及针对近期设备定制的顺序形式，并通过质子-氢电荷转移动力学（一个典型的含时量子化学问题）的数值模拟验证了该方法的有效性。这项工作为从量子-经典混合变分量子算法过渡到针对一般含时哈密顿量（尤其是那些动力学允许紧凑变分描述的体系）的全量子求解器建立了系统化路径，为在含时模拟中实现完全量子计算优势开辟了道路。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> The most widely used approach for simulating the dynamics of time-dependent Hamiltonians via quantum computation depends on the quantum-classical hybrid variational quantum time evolution algorithm, in which ordinary differential equations of the variational coefficients for determining time evolution are solved via classical simulations with a time discretization method. We here present a full-quantum approach, in which ordinary differential equations of the variational coefficients are transformed into static linear equations via the Chebyshev spectral discretization method and then solved via the quantum singular value transformation algorithm. Our full quantum algorithm avoids classical feedback, achieves exponential convergence for smooth Hamiltonians, and yields a quantum circuit depth that is independent of the number of time steps. We demonstrate two implementation strategies, with a global formulation designed for fault-tolerant architectures and a sequential formulation tailored to near-term devices, and validate the approach through numerical simulations of proton-hydrogen charge-transfer dynamics, a prototypical time-dependent quantum chemistry problem. This work establishes a systematic pathway from quantum-classical hybrid variational quantum algorithms to full-quantum solvers for general time-dependent Hamiltonians, particularly those whose dynamics admit compact variational descriptions, opening a route toward full quantum computational advantages in time-dependent simulations.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum computation, time-dependent Hamiltonians, variational quantum algorithms, Chebyshev spectral discretization, quantum singular value transformation, quantum dynamics simulation, quantum chemistry, full-quantum approach

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们采用系统-环境方法，在量子领域中对耗散适应假说进行研究。该假说认为，自组织源于系统耗散其从外部驱动中瞬态吸收的功的能力。我们分析了一个受驱开放系统的量子动力学，该系统由含时自旋-玻色哈密顿量描述，该模型模拟了一个具有可控不对称性的亚稳态双势阱中的粒子。我们探讨了动态势场所提供的功如何与双势阱两个基态之间的跃迁概率相关联。这些研究推动了对受驱自旋-玻色模型的进一步探索，以理解系统的演化及其热力学含义。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We investigate the dissipative adaptation hypothesis in a quantum regime using a system-reservoir approach. This hypothesis proposes that self-organization arises from a system's ability to dissipate the work transiently absorbed from an external drive. We analyze the quantum dynamics of a driven open system described by a time-dependent spin-boson Hamiltonian modeling a particle in a metastable double-well potential with controllable asymmetry. We explore how the work provided by the dynamic potential is related to the transition probability between the two ground states of the double well. These studies motivate further investigations of the driven spin-boson model toward an understanding of the system's evolution and its thermodynamic implications.

</details>
<br>

### 260. ❌ Bell Inequalities for Smells

**作者**: Ricardo Faleiro, Flavien Hirsch, Emmanuel Zambrini Cruzeiro, Nicolas Gisin
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17030v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17030v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

| 关键词 | 权重 | 相关度 | 得分 |
|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文《Bell Inequalities for Smells》研究的是量子物理中的贝尔不等式理论，具体探讨了涉及结果直接相等比较的贝尔不等式类别及其在多方场景中的应用。论文内容完全属于量子信息、量子非定域性和贝尔不等式理论领域，与医学图像分析、深度学习、疾病诊断、手术规划等医疗AI主题没有任何关联。所有评分关键词均与医疗AI相关，而论文研究的是量子物理基础理论，因此所有关键词的相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了一类涉及结果直接相等比较的贝尔不等式，通过定义相应的局部多面体子结构并求解，发现了数千个新的紧致不等式，证明了这些简单不等式可以作为发现新贝尔不等式和设备无关见证者的有力工具。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 本研究探讨了一类特殊的贝尔不等式，其仅涉及结果间的直接等值比较。当实验结果难以表征时，此类不等式自然显现。例如，若测量产生的是气味，单独处理每种气味可能不切实际，但判断两种气味是否相同则仍具可行性。在双体情形中，该场景可视为全关联不等式（异或游戏）向多值输出的自然推广。我们定义了与此场景对应的局域多胞形子结构，并利用其若干结构特性，求解了多个双体及多体场景。通过此方法，我们获得了数千个新的紧致不等式，其中许多同时也是标准局域多胞形的切面。我们还定义了一致性贝尔不等式，这是前述类别在多体场景中的特例，其中仅考虑全等值事件（所有结果均相同）。我们证明此类不等式总可表述为确定性非局域游戏，并给出了一个简单的多体一致性不等式族，证明了其局域界限。研究表明，这些不等式大多允许量子违背，并展示了它们对非局域性研究的重要意义。例如，我们识别出此类不等式可作为维度见证、结果见证、真多体非局域性见证的实例，且与CHSH不等式相关联。这些结果表明，这些简洁而优美的不等式本身为发现新的贝尔不等式和设备无关见证提供了有力工具。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> In this work, we study a particular class of Bell inequalities involving only direct equality-comparisons of outcomes. This arises naturally when outcomes are difficult to characterize. For instance, if measurements yield smells, it may be impractical to process them individually, while still being reasonable to judge whether two smells are identical or not. In the bipartite case, the scenario can be interpreted as a natural generalization of full-correlator inequalities (XOR games) beyond binary outputs. We define the sub-polytope of the local polytope corresponding to this scenario and solve it for several bipartite and multipartite scenarios by leveraging some structural properties. In doing so, we obtain thousands of new tight inequalities, many of which are also facets of the standard local polytope. We also define unanimous Bell inequalities, a particular case of the previous class applied to the multipartite setting in which only full-equality events (all outcomes equal) are considered. We show that such inequalities can always be written as deterministic nonlocal games, and we give a simple multipartite unanimous family and prove its local bound. We show that most of these inequalities admit quantum violations, and we also display aspects of their importance for nonlocality. For instance, we identify examples where such inequalities can act as dimension witnesses, outcome witnesses, witnesses of genuine multipartite nonlocality, as well as being relevant to CHSH. These results show that these simple and elegant inequalities by themselves provide a powerful tool for discovering new Bell inequalities and device-independent witnesses.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Bell inequalities, nonlocality, quantum violations, multipartite scenarios, local polytope, device-independent witnesses, full-correlator inequalities, unanimous Bell inequalities

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了单式量子通道的混合酉性表征问题，通过将其与非马尔可夫动力学中的记忆效应联系起来，开发了基于半定规划的数值高效见证方法，优于现有标准。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 酉量子信道以其保持最大混合态不变的特性定义，构成一类重要的量子操作。其中一类显著子集可表示为幺正演化的概率混合。刻画那些不允许此类分解的信道通常是一个难题，对量子技术中的噪声抑制及量子信息论中的基本问题具有重要影响。本文建立了酉量子信道的混合幺正性与非马尔可夫动力学中记忆效应的（量子）本质之间的联系。通过将问题转化为过程张量的语言，这一关联产生了一个半定规划层次结构，为检测非混合幺正行为提供了数值高效的判据，其性能优于现有标准。我们通过三维和四维酉量子信道的示例，证明了该方法的有效性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Unital quantum channels, defined by their property of leaving the maximally mixed state invariant, form an important class of quantum operations. A distinguished subset of these channels can be represented as a probabilistic mixture of unitary evolutions. Characterizing channels that do not admit such a decomposition is in general a hard problem with significant implications for noise mitigation in quantum technologies and for fundamental problems in quantum information theory. Here we establish a link between mixed-unitarity of unital channels and the (quantum) nature of the memory effects in non-Markovian dynamics. Translating the problem into the language of process tensors, this connection yields a hierarchy of semidefinite programs that provides numerically efficient witnesses for non-mixed-unitary behavior, outperforming existing criteria. We demonstrate the power of this approach through illustrative examples of unital channels in dimensions three and four.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: unital quantum channels, mixed-unitary dynamics, quantum memory, non-Markovian dynamics, process tensors, semidefinite programs, quantum information theory

### 262. ❌ Tumula information and doubly minimized Petz Renyi lautum information

**作者**: Lukas Schmitt, Filippo Girardi, Laura Burri
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子信息论中的相关性度量（tumula information和doubly minimized Petz Renyi lautum information），涉及量子态、相对熵、假设检验等纯理论量子信息概念。所有评分关键词均针对医学影像分析、深度学习医疗应用、临床决策支持等具体医疗AI领域，而该论文完全不涉及任何医学、影像、临床或医疗AI相关内容，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了量子信息论中一种双重最小化的lautum信息变体（称为tumula information）及其Petz Renyi版本，推导了这些相关性度量的一般性质，并提供了在量子态假设检验中的操作解释。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们研究一种双重最小化的劳图姆信息变体——该概念是互信息的逆向类比——其定义为任意乘积态与固定二分量子态之间的最小相对熵；我们将此度量称为图穆拉信息。此外，我们引入了相应的佩茨·伦伊版本，称之为双重最小化佩茨·伦伊劳图姆信息（PRLI）。我们推导了这些关联度量的若干一般性质，并在假设检验的背景下给出了操作解释。具体而言，我们证明某些二元量子态判别问题的反向直接指数由阶数为 $α\in (0,1/2)$ 的双重最小化 PRLI 量化，且萨诺夫指数由图穆拉信息决定。进一步，我们研究了图穆拉信息向信道的扩展，并将其性质与先前关于信道分音信息的研究结果 [Girardi et al., arXiv:2503.21479] 进行了比较。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We study a doubly minimized variant of the lautum information - a reversed analogue of the mutual information - defined as the minimum relative entropy between any product state and a fixed bipartite quantum state; we refer to this measure as the tumula information. In addition, we introduce the corresponding Petz Renyi version, which we call the doubly minimized Petz Renyi lautum information (PRLI). We derive several general properties of these correlation measures and provide an operational interpretation in the context of hypothesis testing. Specifically, we show that the reverse direct exponent of certain binary quantum state discrimination problems is quantified by the doubly minimized PRLI of order $α\in (0,1/2)$, and that the Sanov exponent is determined by the tumula information. Furthermore, we investigate the extension of the tumula information to channels and compare its properties with previous results on the channel umlaut information [Girardi et al., arXiv:2503.21479].

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: tumula information, doubly minimized Petz Renyi lautum information, quantum information theory, relative entropy, quantum state discrimination, hypothesis testing, correlation measures, bipartite quantum state

### 263. ❌ Luttinger's Theorem Violation and Green's Function Topological Invariants in a Fractional Chern Insulator

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 卢廷格定理通过单粒子格林函数的全局性质约束相互作用费米子的粒子密度，其破缺标志着量子化霍尔响应与基于格林函数的石川-松山不变量之间对应关系的失效。这一现象在强关联拓扑相（如分数量子陈绝缘体）中尤为显著，其中分数化准粒子与电子之间缺乏绝热联系，这引发了基于格林函数的拓扑不变量在此类物相中如何显现的问题。通过对费米子哈珀-霍夫施塔特-哈伯德模型进行精确对角化，我们计算了深处于分数量子陈绝缘体相中的体单粒子格林函数，并直接评估了卢廷格计数、其可能的修正项（卢廷格积分）以及石川-松山不变量$N_3[\mathrm{G}]$。我们明确展示了卢廷格定理的破缺，并证明多体陈数的分数特性编码于卢廷格积分的斯特雷达响应中，而整数不变量$N_3[\mathrm{G}]$则源于卢廷格计数的斯特雷达响应。我们进一步通过解析证明：在忽略布洛赫能带混合的情况下，$N_3[\mathrm{G}]$完全由卢廷格计数与被占布洛赫能带的陈数共同决定。最后，我们提出一种实验方案，可通过局域态密度测量提取所有基于格林函数的拓扑不变量，该测量在分数量子霍尔系统中具有实验可行性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Luttinger's theorem constrains the particle density of interacting fermions through global properties of the single-particle Green's function, and its violation signals a breakdown of the identification between the quantized Hall response and the Green-function-based Ishikawa-Matsuyama invariant. This phenomenon becomes especially compelling in strongly correlated topological phases, such as fractional Chern insulators, where fractionalized quasiparticles lack an adiabatic connection to electrons, raising the question of how Green's-function-based topological invariants manifest in such phases. Using exact diagonalization of the fermionic Harper-Hofstadter-Hubbard model, we compute bulk single-particle Green's functions deep inside a fractional Chern insulating phase and directly evaluate the Luttinger count, its possible correction (the Luttinger integral), and the Ishikawa-Matsuyama invariant $N_3[\mathrm{G}]$. We demonstrate a clear violation of Luttinger's theorem and show that the fractional nature of the many-body Chern number is encoded in the Středa response of the Luttinger integral, while the integer invariant $N_3[\mathrm{G}]$ arises from the Středa response of the Luttinger count. We also analytically prove that $N_3[\mathrm{G}]$ is fully determined by the Luttinger count together with the Chern number of the occupied Bloch band, upon neglecting Bloch-band mixing. Finally, we propose an experimental protocol to extract all Green-function-based topological invariants from local density-of-states measurements, experimentally accessible in fractional quantum Hall systems.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Luttinger's theorem, fractional Chern insulator, Green's function topological invariants, Ishikawa-Matsuyama invariant, Harper-Hofstadter-Hubbard model, many-body Chern number, Středa response, local density-of-states

---

### 264. ❌ Kinematic Emergence of the Page Curve in a Local Transverse-Field Ising Model

**作者**: Samuel J. W. Jones, M. Basil Altaie, Benjamin T. H. Varcoe

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文通过可控的量子自旋链模型模拟黑洞蒸发过程，展示了仅通过子系统尺寸的动力学缩减即可产生Page曲线行为，揭示了内部信息动力学对曲线形状的影响。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们提出一种可控量子自旋链模型，该模型仅通过局域相互作用与子系统尺寸的动力学缩减，即可复现黑洞蒸发过程中预期的二分纠缠度先升后降的佩奇曲线特征。该模型将两条横场伊辛链耦合形成纯二分态：通过动态收缩“系统”链并扩展“环境”链来模拟类霍金蒸发过程，同时利用矩阵乘积态张量网络进行幺正实时演化模拟。在此受控子系统尺寸调节下，佩奇曲线的特征轮廓稳定显现；值得注意的是，即使将边界处显式的哈密顿量耦合设为零，该曲线依然存在，这证明仅通过希尔伯特空间维度的收缩即可产生佩奇曲线行为。我们进一步揭示曲线的具体形态取决于体系内部的信息动力学：在临界点附近操作时曲线呈现平滑轮廓，而偏离临界状态则会扭曲纠缠的增长与衰减过程。这些研究结果将局域相互作用的自旋链确立为可在当前量子硬件上探索黑洞启发的信息动力学的现实平台。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We present a controllable quantum spin-chain model that reproduces the Page curve (the rise-and-fall of bipartite entanglement expected in black-hole evaporation), using only local interactions and a kinematic reduction of the subsystem size. Two transverse-field Ising chains are coupled to form a pure bipartite state; Hawking-like evaporation is implemented by dynamically shrinking the 'system' chain and enlarging the 'environment' chain, while unitary real-time evolution is simulated with matrix product state (MPS) tensor networks. The characteristic Page curve profile emerges robustly under this controlled subsystem resizing and notably persists even when the explicit Hamiltonian coupling across the boundary is set to zero, demonstrating that shrinking Hilbert-space dimension alone can generate Page curve behaviour. We show that the detailed shape of the curve depends on the internal information dynamics: operation at criticality yields a smooth profile, whereas moving away from criticality distorts entanglement growth and decay. These results position locally interacting spin chains as a realistic platform for probing black-hole-inspired information dynamics on current quantum hardware.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Page curve, quantum spin-chain, transverse-field Ising model, black-hole evaporation, bipartite entanglement, matrix product state, information dynamics, criticality

### 265. ❌ Chiral and bond-ordered phases in a triangular-ladder superconducting-qubit quantum simulator

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究利用超导量子比特模拟三角梯状晶格上的玻色-哈伯德模型，通过调控耦合参数和合成磁通，观测到了手性超流体、迈斯纳超流体和键序绝缘体等量子物相的特征。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 强相互作用多体系统常展现出在单粒子或无相互作用极限中明显缺失的宏观行为。此类涌现现象在晶格哈伯德模型中得到了充分体现，其中相互作用、几何阻挫与磁通之间的耦合催生了丰富的物理内容。超导量子比特天然地实现了玻色-哈伯德模型的类比量子模拟，同时提供了可调参数、格点分辨控制以及快速的实验重复率。本文研究了一种在三角梯子晶格上实现玻色-哈伯德模型的超导量子比特器件。通过调节耦合的强度与符号，我们构建了合成磁通以表征不同参数区间下对应的半填充基态。我们测量了类比于电流-电流关联算符与键动能的可观测量，发现了与手征超流体、迈斯纳超流体及键有序绝缘体相一致的特征。本研究确立了超导电路作为一个可稳健探测阻挫玻色-哈伯德系统中量子物相的平台，即使在强关联无能隙区间亦适用。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Many-body systems with strong interactions often exhibit macroscopic behavior markedly absent in single-particle or noninteracting limits. Such emergent phenomena are well exemplified in lattice Hubbard models, where the interplay between interactions, geometric frustration, and magnetic flux gives rise to rich physics. Superconducting qubits naturally enable analog quantum simulation of Bose-Hubbard models, while offering tunable parameters, site-resolved control, and rapid experimental repetition rates. Here, we study a superconducting-qubit device that realizes the Bose-Hubbard model on a triangular-ladder lattice. By tuning the magnitude and sign of couplings, we engineer a synthetic magnetic flux to characterize the resulting half-filling ground state for various parameter regimes. We measure observables analogous to current-current correlators and bond kinetic energies, finding signatures consistent with chiral superfluids, Meissner superfluids, and bond-ordered insulators. Our results establish superconducting circuits as a platform for robustly probing quantum phases of matter in frustrated Bose-Hubbard systems, even in strongly correlated and gapless regimes.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: superconducting qubits, Bose-Hubbard model, triangular-ladder lattice, chiral superfluids, bond-ordered insulators, quantum simulation, synthetic magnetic flux

### 266. ❌ The Algebraic Landscape of Kochen-Specker Sets in Dimension Three

**作者**: Michael Kernaghan
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16988v1](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16988v1)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是量子力学中的Kochen-Specker定理和希尔伯特空间中的数学结构，属于理论物理和数学领域，与医学图像分析、人工智能临床决策支持等医学应用主题完全无关。所有关键词均未在标题或摘要中出现，也没有任何间接关联。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文通过计算调查了三维希尔伯特空间中Kochen-Specker不可着色集在不同代数字母表下的出现条件，发现它们仅由两种代数抵消机制产生，并识别出六个离散的代数岛屿，其中两个可能对应新的KS图类型。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们对三维希尔伯特空间中基于二值坐标字母表$\mathcal{A} = \{0, \pm 1, \pm x\}$的Kochen-Specker（KS）不可着色性进行了计算性研究，其中字母表取自二次域、分圆域和黄金比例数域。在所有测试的字母表中，仅当$x$支持两种抵消机制之一时才会出现KS集：模-2抵消（生成元满足$|x|^2 = 2$，例如$|\sqrt{2}|^2=2$、$|\sqrt{-2}|^2=2$或$|α|^2=2$；整数情形$1+1=2$是退化的加法实例）或相位抵消（单位模项之和为零，如$1+ω+ω^2=0$）。在我们的研究中，生成元满足$|x|^2 \geq 3$且非单位根的字母表仅产生正交三元组，而未出现KS不可着色性。这一经验规律解释了为何在测试的数域中，构造会聚集为六个离散的代数岛。其中两个岛屿产生了潜在的新型KS图类型：Heegner-7环$\mathbb{Z}[(1+\sqrt{-7})/2]$（43个向量）和黄金比例域$\mathbb{Q}(\varphi)$（52个向量，仅通过叉积完备化揭示）；$\mathbb{Z}[\sqrt{-2}]$则为已知的Peres型图提供了新的代数实现。利用基于SAT（可满足性）的二部KS不可着色性方法，我们验证并扩展了Trandafir和Cabello对所有六个代数岛中二部完美量子策略的输入计数。这两种机制的模式是否可推广至所有数域，仍是一个开放问题。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We present a computational survey of Kochen-Specker (KS) uncolorability in three-dimensional Hilbert space across two-symbol coordinate alphabets $\mathcal{A} = \{0, \pm 1, \pm x\}$ drawn from quadratic, cyclotomic, and golden-ratio number fields. In every tested alphabet, KS sets arise only when $x$ supports one of two cancellation mechanisms: modulus-2 cancellation (the generator satisfies $|x|^2 = 2$, as in $|\sqrt{2}|^2=2$, $|\sqrt{-2}|^2=2$, or $|α|^2=2$; the integer case $1+1=2$ is the degenerate additive instance) or phase cancellation (a vanishing sum of unit-modulus terms, as in $1+ω+ω^2=0$). Alphabets whose generators have $|x|^2 \geq 3$ and are not roots of unity produce orthogonal triples but not KS-uncolorability in our survey. This empirical pattern explains why constructions cluster into six discrete algebraic islands among the tested fields. Two yield potentially new KS graph types: the Heegner-7 ring $\mathbb{Z}[(1+\sqrt{-7})/2]$ (43 vectors) and the golden ratio field $\mathbb{Q}(\varphi)$ (52 vectors, revealed only by cross-product completion); $\mathbb{Z}[\sqrt{-2}]$ provides a new algebraic realization of a known Peres-type graph. Using SAT-based bipartite KS-uncolorability, we verify and extend the input counts of Trandafir and Cabello for bipartite perfect quantum strategies across all six islands. Whether the two-mechanism pattern extends to all number fields remains an open question.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Kochen-Specker sets, Hilbert space, algebraic cancellation, quantum uncolorability, number fields, SAT-based verification, orthogonal triples, graph types

### 267. ❌ Measurement-Based Estimation of Causal Conditional Variances and Its Application to Macroscopic quantum phenomenon

**作者**: Kosei Hatakeyama, Ryotaro Fukuzumi, Akira Matsumura, Daisuke Miki, Kazuhiro Yamamoto
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究基于测量记录的量子因果条件方差估计方法，并证明在典型量子态制备参数下重构偏差可忽略，应用于宏观量子纠缠和压缩态验证。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们在C.Meng等人（《科学进展》8, 7585 (2022)）所建立的理论框架基础上，对一种基于离腔（detuned cavity）系统中机械振子的量子估计方法进行了分析研究，该方法仅依赖于零差测量（homodyne measurement）记录。仅基于测量记录的估计具有重要意义，因为它能在不预设真实系统状态知识的前提下实现量子态验证。我们通过因果与反因果量子维纳滤波器（quantum Wiener filters）构建了一个相对估计算子，并计算了其方差。将结果与因果条件方差之间的偏差定义为重构偏差，我们对其大小进行了解析评估。研究表明，在典型量子态制备实验相关的参数范围内，重构偏差足够小，可以忽略不计。作为量子态验证的应用示例，我们将该方法应用于两项提案：一是电磁相互作用介导的宏观量子纠缠方案，二是通过零差检测产生的条件动量压缩态（conditional momentum-squeezed states）方案，从而明确了重构偏差可忽略的条件以及偏差变得显著的情形。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We analytically investigate a quantum estimation method for a mechanical oscillator in a detuned cavity system based solely on homodyne measurement records, building on the framework developed by C.Meng et al. (Science Advances 8, 7585 (2022)). Estimation based only on measurement records is important because it enables state verification without assuming knowledge of the true system state. We construct a relative estimate operator from causal and anti-causal quantum Wiener filters and calculate its variance. The deviation from the causal conditional variance is defined as a reconstruction bias, whose magnitude is evaluated analytically. We show that, within experimentally relevant parameter regimes for typical quantum-state preparation, the reconstruction bias is sufficiently small to be neglected. As applications to state verification, we apply the method to proposals for macroscopic quantum entanglement mediated by electromagnetic interactions and for conditional momentum-squeezed states generated by homodyne detection, and clarify the conditions under which the bias remains negligible and when the reconstruction bias becomes significant.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum estimation, causal conditional variance, homodyne measurement, quantum Wiener filters, reconstruction bias, macroscopic quantum entanglement, quantum-state verification, mechanical oscillator

### 268. ❌ High-rate quantum digital signatures over 250 km of optical fiber

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了量子数字签名在长距离光纤网络中签名率低和信道损耗容忍度差的问题，通过结合Sagnac干涉仪的相位稳定偏振调制、GHz速率量子态编码和超导纳米线单光子探测器，实现了比现有系统高两个数量级的签名率，并在高达49.05 dB信道损耗下保持每秒约1.25次的有效签名率。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子数字签名（Quantum Digital Signatures, QDS）为消息完整性、真实性与不可否认性提供了信息论安全性，是未来量子网络的基础密码学原语。尽管已取得显著进展，但QDS的实际部署一直受到签名速率有限和信道损耗容忍度低的严重制约，尤其是在长距离和城域规模的网络中。本文报道了一种高速率、抗损耗的QDS系统，同时克服了这两个关键瓶颈。我们的实现结合了基于萨格纳克干涉仪的固有相位稳定偏振调制、千兆赫兹速率的量子态编码以及低时间抖动的超导纳米线单光子探测器，从而能够在高重复频率下实现稳健且连续的运行。通过将该硬件平台与基于一次性通用哈希的QDS协议相结合，在可比信道损耗条件下，我们实现的签名速率较现有QDS方案提高了两个数量级以上。值得注意的是，在总信道损耗高达49.05 dB时，系统仍能保持约每秒1.25次的有效签名速率，这是迄今报道的QDS最高损耗容忍度。这些结果为在实际量子通信网络中部署QDS建立了一条实用且可扩展的技术路径。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum digital signatures (QDS) offer information-theoretic security for message integrity, authenticity, and non-repudiation, and constitute a fundamental cryptographic primitive for future quantum networks. Despite significant progress, the practical deployment of QDS has been severely constrained by limited signature rates and poor tolerance to channel loss, particularly in long-distance and metropolitan-scale networks. Here, we report a high-rate, loss-resilient QDS system that overcomes these two key bottlenecks simultaneously. Our implementation combines intrinsically phase-stable polarization modulation based on a Sagnac interferometer with gigahertz-rate quantum state encoding and low-timing-jitter superconducting nanowire single-photon detectors, enabling robust and continuous operation at high repetition frequencies. By integrating this hardware platform with a one-time universal hashing-based QDS protocol, we achieve a signature rate improvement of more than two orders of magnitude compared with existing QDS implementations under comparable channel-loss conditions. Notably, the system maintains a non-zero effective signature rate of approximately 1.25 times per second at a total channel loss of up to 49.05 dB, representing the highest loss tolerance reported for QDS to date. These results establish a practical and scalable technological pathway for deploying QDS in real-world quantum communication networks.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum digital signatures, optical fiber communication, Sagnac interferometer, superconducting nanowire single-photon detectors, channel loss tolerance, quantum state encoding, information-theoretic security, quantum networks

### 269. ❌ Spin entanglement signatures of proton from a light-front Hamiltonian

**作者**: Chen Qian, Siqi Xu, Yang-Guang Yang, Xingbo Zhao
**期刊/来源**: arxiv

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究比较了Basis Light-Front Quantization和夸克-双夸克模型中质子自旋纠缠的差异，发现夸克-双夸克模型在价费克扇区产生更强的纠缠态，主要源于更大的W型和贝尔型纠缠。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子纠缠为强子的内部结构提供了定量探针，并为研究强子波函数中的量子关联提供了灵敏手段。对于重子而言，三个价夸克的自旋态构成了一个三方量子比特系统，其纠缠结构可通过三类三量子比特态进行表征。本研究将基于基矢光前量子化（Basis Light-Front Quantization, BLFQ）获得的质子自旋纠缠与夸克-双夸克模型的结果进行比较。通过分析双方纠缠与三方纠缠，我们发现夸克-双夸克模型在价福克（valence Fock）扇区中产生的自旋态纠缠程度显著高于BLFQ波函数。这一差异主要源于夸克-双夸克模型中更强的W型与贝尔型纠缠。在BLFQ框架内，较大的强耦合常数与较小的夸克质量会驱使价夸克间的自旋关联趋向于一种有效的夸克-双夸克构型，其中包含一个活跃的$d$夸克与一个关联的$uu$夸克对。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum entanglement provides a quantitative probe of the internal structure of hadrons and offers a sensitive means to study the quantum correlation in the hadron wave functions. For baryons, the spin state of the three valence quarks forms a tripartite qubit system, whose entanglement structure can be characterized by the four classes of three-qubit states. In this work, we compare the proton spin entanglement obtained from Basis Light-Front Quantization (BLFQ) with that from a quark-diquark model. By analyzing both bipartite and tripartite entanglement, we find that the quark-diquark model yields a substantially more entangled spin state than the BLFQ wave function in the valence Fock sector. This difference mainly originates from the larger W-type and Bell-type entanglement in the quark-diquark model. Within BLFQ, larger stronger coupling constant and smaller quark mass drive the spin correlation among the valence quarks towards an effective quark-diquark configuration with an active $d$ quark and a correlated $uu$ pair.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum entanglement, proton spin, Basis Light-Front Quantization, quark-diquark model, three-qubit states, hadron wave functions, spin correlation, valence quarks

**作者**: Baptiste Claudon, Alexis Lucas, Jean-Philip Piquemal, César Feniou, Julien Zylberman

**评分理由**: 论文研究量子计算中的量子态制备方法，特别是针对多项式振幅的量子态，使用对数深度电路和线性辅助量子比特。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析、深度学习、AI诊断、预后预测、手术规划等医学应用领域，而论文内容完全聚焦于量子算法、量子电路设计和量子计算理论，与医学影像或临床决策支持没有任何关联。因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种使用对数深度量子电路高效制备多项式振幅量子态的新方法，通过改进的线性组合酉算子和广义量子特征值变换技术，在14量子比特的离子阱处理器上实现了原理验证。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 量子态制备是众多量子算法中的核心基本操作，但其通常需要大量资源，目前仅对具有特定结构的态族已知高效的制备方案。本研究提出了一种制备量子态的方法，该态的振幅由$d$次多项式给出，所使用电路的深度随量子比特数$n$呈对数增长，且仅需$\mathcal O(n)$个辅助量子比特，这改进了先前需要线性深度电路的方法。该方案首先基于泡利基分解，构建了一个仿射对角算子的块编码，该分解仅涉及$n$项。我们引入了一种改进的酉算子线性组合技术，以对数深度实现此分解，同时提出了一种新颖的EXACT-one预言机电路，用于标记其中恰好有一个量子比特处于$|1\rangle$态的计算基态。随后，该方法利用广义量子本征值变换将这一仿射算子提升为任意次数的多项式。文中报告了理论分析和数值模拟结果，并在一个囚禁离子量子处理器上进行了原理验证性实现，使用了$14$个量子比特和超过$500$个基本量子门。由于多项式近似在科学计算中无处不在，此方案为量子态制备提供了一种可扩展且资源高效的方法，进一步提升了量子算法在化学、物理、工程和金融等领域的潜力。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Quantum state preparation is a central primitive in many quantum algorithms, yet it is generally resource intensive, with efficient constructions known only for structured families of states. This work introduces a method for preparing quantum states whose amplitudes are given by a degree$-d$ polynomial, using circuits with logarithmic depth in the number $n$ of qubits and only $\mathcal O(n)$ ancilla qubits, improving previous approaches that required linear-depth circuits. The construction first relies on a block-encoding of an affine diagonal operator based on its Pauli-basis decomposition, which involves only $n$ terms. A modified linear-combination-of-unitaries (LCU) technique is introduced to implement this decomposition in logarithmic depth, together with a novel circuit for the EXACT-one oracle that flags basis states in which exactly one qubit is in the state $|1\rangle$. It then uses a generalized quantum eigenvalue transformation (GQET) to promote this affine operator to an arbitrary degree polynomial. Theoretical analysis and numerical simulations are reported along with a proof-of-principle implementation on a trapped-ion quantum processor using $14$ qubits and more than $500$ primitive quantum gates. Because polynomial approximations are ubiquitous in scientific computing, this construction provides a scalable and resource-efficient approach to quantum state preparation, further improving the potential of quantum algorithms in fields such as chemistry, physics, engineering, and finance.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum state preparation, logarithmic-depth circuits, polynomial amplitudes, linear-combination-of-unitaries, quantum eigenvalue transformation, quantum algorithms, quantum computing, trapped-ion quantum processor

### 271. ❌ Uncertainty Relation for Entropy and Temperature of Gibbs States

**作者**: Francis J. Headley
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17

| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文标题为《Uncertainty Relation for Entropy and Temperature of Gibbs States》，摘要内容完全围绕量子热力学、吉布斯态、熵估计、费舍尔信息、不确定性关系等理论物理和统计力学概念展开。所有评分关键词均涉及医学影像分析、人工智能临床决策支持等应用领域，而该论文是纯理论物理研究，两者在研究对象、方法、应用场景上没有任何交集。因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文研究了吉布斯态中熵与温度的不确定性关系，推导出熵估计的量子费舍尔信息与温度费舍尔信息之间的对偶关系，并证明了一个与系统具体细节无关的普适不确定性关系。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 我们推导了吉布斯态中熵估计的量子费舍尔信息，并证明其满足 $F_s = 1/C_v$，与温度的费舍尔信息 $F_S = C_v/T^2$ 构成对偶关系。二者的乘积 $F_S\cdot F_T = 1/T^2$ 与哈密顿量无关，从而导出一个普适的不确定关系 $Δ^2 S\,Δ^2 T \geq T^2/n^2$，其中所有与系统相关的量——如热容、哈密顿量以及自由度数目——均完全抵消。这是熵 $S$ 与温度 $T$ 之间勒让德共轭性的度量学表达。我们确认能量测量是熵估计的最优方案，分析了临界点标度行为（其中 $F_S \sim |t|^α\to 0$），并将 $F_S$ 与熵坐标下的鲁佩纳度规联系起来。该不确定关系被证明对所有标准热力学共轭对均成立，并探讨了冯·诺依曼熵在雷尼熵族中的特殊地位。最后，我们将结论推广至巨正则系综和广义吉布斯系综。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> We derive the quantum Fisher information for entropy estimation in a Gibbs state and show that $F_s = 1/C_v$, dual to the temperature Fisher information $F_S = C_v/T^2$. Their product $F_S\cdot F_T = 1/T^2$ is independent of the Hamiltonian, yielding the universal uncertainty relation $Δ^2 S\,Δ^2 T \geq T^2/n^2$ in which all system-specific quantities such as heat capacity, the Hamiltonian, and the number of degrees of freedom cancel identically. This is the metrological expression of the Legendre conjugacy between $S$ and $T$. We identify energy measurement as the optimal protocol for entropy estimation, analyse critical-point scaling where $F_S \sim |t|^α\to 0$, and connect $F_S$ to the Ruppeiner metric in entropy coordinates. The uncertainty relation is shown to hold for all standard thermodynamic conjugate pairs, and we examine the distinguished role of the von~Neumann entropy within the Rényi family. Generalisations to the grand canonical and generalised Gibbs ensembles are given.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: Gibbs states, entropy estimation, quantum Fisher information, uncertainty relation, temperature, thermodynamic conjugate pairs, von Neumann entropy, Rényi entropy

---

### 272. ❌ Chipmunq: A Fault-Tolerant Compiler for Chiplet Quantum Architectures

**作者**: Peter Wegmann, Aleksandra Świerkowska, Emmanouil Giortamis, Pramod Bhatotia
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16389v2](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16389v2)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

<details>
<summary>评分详情</summary>

|------|------|------|------|
| medical image analysis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| medical image segmentation | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| deep learning medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| AI for diagnosis | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| prognosis prediction | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| surgical planning | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| multimodal medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |
| foundation models medical imaging | 1.0 | 0.0/10 | 0.0 |

**评分理由**: 论文《Chipmunq: A Fault-Tolerant Compiler for Chiplet Quantum Architectures》专注于量子计算领域，研究量子芯片架构的编译器设计，涉及量子纠错、芯片间互联、电路映射等主题。所有评分关键词均围绕医学影像分析、AI辅助诊断、手术规划等医疗AI应用，与论文的量子计算研究方向完全无关，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了在模块化量子芯片架构上编译容错量子电路的难题，提出了Chipmunq编译器，通过量子纠错感知的分区策略显著提升了编译效率、减少了电路深度和SWAP门数量，并改善了逻辑错误率。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 随着量子计算通过量子纠错向容错方向演进，模块化芯粒架构应运而生，以提供所需的大规模量子比特数，同时克服单片芯片的制造限制。然而，这一转变引发了一个关键的编译鸿沟：现有框架无法在管理芯粒后端噪声大、连接稀疏特性的同时，处理容错量子电路的规模。
> 
> 我们提出Chipmunq，这是首个面向硬件、能将容错量子电路映射并路由至模块化架构的编译器。Chipmunq采用一种量子纠错感知的分区策略，该策略能保持逻辑量子比特补丁的完整性，从而避免了通用编译器中常见的、代价高昂的门开销。我们的评估表明，与最先进工具相比，Chipmunq实现了13.5倍的编译时间加速。通过纳入芯粒约束和缺陷量子比特，它在不同代码距离下将电路深度降低了86.4%，SWAP门数量减少了91.4%。至关重要的是，Chipmunq克服了芯粒间异构连接的问题，将逻辑错误率提升高达两个数量级。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> As quantum computing advances toward fault-tolerance through quantum error correction, modular chiplet architectures have emerged to provide the massive qubit counts required while overcoming fabrication limits of monolithic chips. However, this transition introduces a critical compilation gap: existing frameworks cannot handle the scale of fault-tolerant quantum circuits while managing the noisy, sparse interconnects of chiplet backends.
>   We present Chipmunq, the first hardware-aware compiler for mapping and routing fault-tolerant circuits onto modular architectures. Chipmunq employs a quantum-error-correction-aware partitioning strategy that preserves the integrity of logical qubit patches, preventing prohibitive gate overheads common in general-purpose compilers. Our evaluation demonstrates that Chipmunq achieves a 13.5x speedup in compilation time compared to state-of-the-art tools. By incorporating chiplet constraints and defective qubits, it reduces circuit depth by 86.4% and SWAP gate counts by 91.4% across varying code distances. Crucially, Chipmunq overcomes heterogeneous inter-chiplet links, improving logical error rates by up to two orders of magnitude.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: quantum computing, fault-tolerant compiler, chiplet architectures, quantum error correction, circuit mapping, logical qubit patches, inter-chiplet links, SWAP gate reduction

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 基于学习的语义通信（SemCom）近期已成为提升无线网络传输效率的前沿范式。然而，现有方法通常依赖于大量端到端训练，这在动态无线环境中既缺乏灵活性又计算成本高昂。此外，这些方法未能利用语义相似内容多次传输中的冗余性，限制了整体效率。为克服这些局限，我们提出一种基于信道感知生成对抗网络（GAN）反演的联合信源信道编码（CAGI-JSCC）框架，该框架通过利用预训练的语义风格生成对抗网络（SemanticStyleGAN）模型实现免训练的语义通信。通过将无线信道特性显式地融入GAN反演过程，CAGI-JSCC无需额外训练即可适应变化的信道条件。进一步，我们设计了一种支持缓存的动态码本（CDC），在发射端与接收端缓存解耦的语义组件，使系统能够复用先前传输的内容。这种语义级缓存可随经验积累持续减少冗余传输。在图像传输任务上的大量实验验证了所提框架的有效性。特别地，我们的系统在平均带宽压缩比（BCR）为1/224时达到可比的感知质量，单幅图像传输的BCR可低至1/1024，显著优于基准方法（BCR为1/128）。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Learning-based semantic communication (SemCom) has recently emerged as a promising paradigm for improving the transmission efficiency of wireless networks. However, existing methods typically rely on extensive end-to-end training, which is both inflexible and computationally expensive in dynamic wireless environments. Moreover, they fail to exploit redundancy across multiple transmissions of semantically similar content, limiting overall efficiency. To overcome these limitations, we propose a channel-aware generative adversarial network (GAN) inversion-based joint source-channel coding (CAGI-JSCC) framework that enables training-free SemCom by leveraging a pre-trained SemanticStyleGAN model. By explicitly incorporating wireless channel characteristics into the GAN inversion process, CAGI-JSCC adapts to varying channel conditions without additional training. Furthermore, we introduce a cache-enabled dynamic codebook (CDC) that caches disentangled semantic components at both the transmitter and receiver, allowing the system to reuse previously transmitted content. This semantic-level caching can continuously reduce redundant transmissions as experience accumulates. Extensive experiments on image transmission demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework. In particular, our system achieves comparable perceptual quality with an average bandwidth compression ratio (BCR) of 1/224, and as low as 1/1024 for a single image, significantly outperforming baselines with a BCR of 1/128.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: semantic communication, joint source-channel coding, GAN inversion, wireless transmission, cache mechanism, bandwidth compression, image transmission, training-free

---

### 274. ❌ A 3D Reconstruction Benchmark for Asset Inspection

**作者**: James L. Gray, Nikolai Goncharov, Alexandre Cardaillac, Ryan Griffiths, Jack Naylor, Donald G. Dansereau

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 资产管理需要精确的三维模型，以支持建筑物、船舶及其他关键结构在老化过程中的维护、修复与评估工作。这些下游应用依赖于通过近距离航空勘测生成的高保真模型，使操作者能够定位并表征结构劣化或损伤，进而规划修复方案。采集的图像通常在相邻相机位姿间具有高重叠度，能呈现毫米级的充足细节，并包含反射与透明等具有挑战性的视觉外观。然而，现有三维重建数据集缺乏此类场景的示例，导致难以对该任务的方法进行基准测试。本文提出一个包含真实深度图、相机位姿和网格模型的新数据集，其中包含三个合成场景，模拟了非朗伯表面内容在检测轨迹和不同表面状态条件下的情况。我们基于该数据集评估了当前先进的重建方法。结果表明，现有方法在处理该领域固有的密集采集轨迹和复杂表面条件时存在显著困难，这揭示了关键的可扩展性差距，并为资产检测中可部署三维重建技术指明了新的研究方向。项目页面：https://roboticimaging.org/Projects/asset-inspection-dataset/

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Asset management requires accurate 3D models to inform the maintenance, repair, and assessment of buildings, maritime vessels, and other key structures as they age. These downstream applications rely on high-fidelity models produced from aerial surveys in close proximity to the asset, enabling operators to locate and characterise deterioration or damage and plan repairs. Captured images typically have high overlap between adjacent camera poses, sufficient detail at millimetre scale, and challenging visual appearances such as reflections and transparency. However, existing 3D reconstruction datasets lack examples of these conditions, making it difficult to benchmark methods for this task. We present a new dataset with ground truth depth maps, camera poses, and mesh models of three synthetic scenes with simulated inspection trajectories and varying levels of surface condition on non-Lambertian scene content. We evaluate state-of-the-art reconstruction methods on this dataset. Our results demonstrate that current approaches struggle significantly with the dense capture trajectories and complex surface conditions inherent to this domain, exposing a critical scalability gap and pointing toward new research directions for deployable 3D reconstruction in asset inspection. Project page: https://roboticimaging.org/Projects/asset-inspection-dataset/

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: 3D reconstruction, asset inspection, benchmark dataset, depth maps, camera poses, mesh models, synthetic scenes, computer vision

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种紧凑型无透镜偏振相机，通过结合衍射器和偏振掩模的光学设计以及计算重建算法，实现了从单次快照中恢复四个线性偏振图像，展示了无透镜方法在偏振成像中的潜力。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 偏振成像是一种生成场景偏振态像素图的技术。尽管人眼无法直接感知偏振信息，但它能够辅助多种传感与计算机视觉任务。现有的偏振相机采用空间或时间复用技术，但这会增加相机的体积、重量、成本或全部上述因素。近年来，无透镜成像方法（如DiffuserCam）已证明，通过用编码元件替代镜头并进行计算重建，可以实现紧凑的成像系统。在本研究中，我们提出了一种由漫射器和简易条纹偏振掩模组成的紧凑型无透镜偏振相机。通过将这种光学设计与一种显式建模偏振编码无透镜测量的重建算法相结合，我们能够从单次快照中重建出四幅线性偏振图像。我们的研究结果展示了无透镜方法在偏振成像领域的潜力，并揭示了影响重建质量的关键物理因素，为开发高质量实用化系统提供了指导。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Polarization imaging is a technique that creates a pixel map of the polarization state in a scene. Although invisible to the human eye, polarization can assist various sensing and computer vision tasks. Existing polarization cameras use spatial or temporal multiplexing, which increases the camera volume, weight, cost, or all of the above. Recent lensless imaging approaches, such as DiffuserCam, have demonstrated that compact imaging systems can be realized by replacing the lens with a coding element and performing computational reconstruction. In this work, we propose a compact lensless polarization camera composed of a diffuser and a simple striped polarization mask. By combining this optical design with a reconstruction algorithm that explicitly models the polarization-encoded lensless measurements, four linear polarization images are recovered from a single snapshot. Our results demonstrate the potential of lensless approaches for polarization imaging and reveal the physical factors that govern reconstruction quality, guiding the development of high-quality practical systems.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: lensless imaging, polarization imaging, computational reconstruction, diffuser, polarization mask, compact camera, optical design, single snapshot

### 276. ❌ Topology-Preserving Deep Joint Source-Channel Coding for Semantic Communication

**作者**: Omar Erak, Omar Alhussein, Fang Fang, Sami Muhaidat

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是无线视觉应用（如自动驾驶）中的拓扑保持深度联合信源信道编码（TopoJSCC），通过持久同调正则化器来保护图像的结构连通性。虽然涉及深度学习、图像重建和鲁棒性，但所有内容都针对通用无线通信场景，没有提及任何医学图像、临床决策、疾病诊断、手术规划或医疗数据。论文与给定的医学图像分析关键词完全无关。

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文针对无线视觉应用中现有深度联合信源信道编码方案缺乏拓扑保护的问题，提出了一个集成持久同调正则化器的拓扑感知框架（TopoJSCC），在低信噪比和带宽比条件下实现了更好的拓扑保持和峰值信噪比。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 许多无线视觉应用（如自动驾驶）需要保持全局结构信息，而不仅仅是逐像素的保真度。然而，现有的深度联合信源信道编码（DeepJSCC）方案主要优化像素级损失，未对连通性或拓扑结构提供显式保护。本文提出TopoJSCC，一种拓扑感知的深度联合信源信道编码框架，该框架将持久同调正则化器集成到端到端训练中。具体而言，我们通过惩罚原始图像与重建图像的立方体持久图之间的Wasserstein距离，以及信道前后潜在特征的Vietoris–Rips持久图之间的Wasserstein距离，以增强拓扑一致性，从而促进鲁棒的潜在流形。TopoJSCC基于端到端学习，无需额外边信息。实验表明，在低信噪比（SNR）和低带宽比条件下，该方法在拓扑保持和峰值信噪比（PSNR）方面均有所提升。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Many wireless vision applications, such as autonomous driving, require preservation of global structural information rather than only per-pixel fidelity. However, existing Deep joint source-channel coding (DeepJSCC) schemes mainly optimize pixel-wise losses and provide no explicit protection of connectivity or topology. This letter proposes TopoJSCC, a topology-aware DeepJSCC framework that integrates persistent-homology regularizers to end-to-end training. Specifically, we enforce topological consistency by penalizing Wasserstein distances between cubical persistence diagrams of original and reconstructed images, and between Vietoris--Rips persistence of latent features before and after the channel to promote a robust latent manifold. TopoJSCC is based on end-to-end learning and requires no side information. Experiments show improved topology preservation and peak signal-to-noise ratio (PSNR) in low signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) and bandwidth-ratio regimes.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: deep joint source-channel coding, topology preservation, persistent homology, semantic communication, wireless vision applications, end-to-end learning, Wasserstein distance, cubical persistence diagrams

### 277. ❌ Leveraging Large Vision Model for Multi-UAV Co-perception in Low-Altitude Wireless Networks

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文提出了一种基于大型视觉模型和深度强化学习的通信高效多无人机协同感知框架，在资源受限的无线环境下显著提升了感知性能并大幅降低了通信开销。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 多无人机协同感知已成为低空经济多样化应用中极具前景的范式，其通过无线通信融合互补的多视角观测以提升感知性能。然而，多无人机产生的大规模视觉数据在通信延迟与资源效率方面带来了严峻挑战。为应对这些挑战，本文提出一种通信高效的协同感知框架，称为基站辅助无人机框架，该框架在提升感知性能的同时降低了通信开销。具体而言，我们采用Top-K选择机制从无人机捕获的RGB图像中识别信息量最高的像素，实现稀疏化视觉传输，从而减少数据量与延迟。稀疏化图像通过多用户MIMO传输至地面服务器，其中基于Swin-large架构的MaskDINO编码器提取鸟瞰图特征，并执行协同特征融合以完成地面车辆感知任务。此外，我们开发了一种基于扩散模型的深度强化学习算法，以联合选择协同无人机、稀疏化比率与预编码矩阵，从而在通信效率与感知效用间取得平衡。在Air-Co-Pred数据集上的仿真结果表明，相较于传统的基于CNN的鸟瞰图融合基线方法，所提出的基站辅助无人机框架在降低85%通信开销的同时，将感知性能提升超过5%，为资源受限无线环境下的多无人机协同感知提供了有效解决方案。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Multi-uncrewed aerial vehicle (UAV) cooperative perception has emerged as a promising paradigm for diverse low-altitude economy applications, where complementary multi-view observations are leveraged to enhance perception performance via wireless communications. However, the massive visual data generated by multiple UAVs poses significant challenges in terms of communication latency and resource efficiency. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a communication-efficient cooperative perception framework, termed Base-Station-Helped UAV (BHU), which reduces communication overhead while enhancing perception performance. Specifically, we employ a Top-K selection mechanism to identify the most informative pixels from UAV-captured RGB images, enabling sparsified visual transmission with reduced data volume and latency. The sparsified images are transmitted to a ground server via multi-user MIMO (MU-MIMO), where a Swin-large-based MaskDINO encoder extracts bird's-eye-view (BEV) features and performs cooperative feature fusion for ground vehicle perception. Furthermore, we develop a diffusion model-based deep reinforcement learning (DRL) algorithm to jointly select cooperative UAVs, sparsification ratios, and precoding matrices, achieving a balance between communication efficiency and perception utility. Simulation results on the Air-Co-Pred dataset demonstrate that, compared with traditional CNN-based BEV fusion baselines, the proposed BHU framework improves perception performance by over 5% while reducing communication overhead by 85%, providing an effective solution for multi-UAV cooperative perception under resource-constrained wireless environments.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: multi-UAV cooperative perception, communication-efficient framework, large vision model, deep reinforcement learning, bird's-eye-view feature fusion, wireless networks, resource-constrained environments, perception performance improvement

### 278. ❌ Intermitotic timing and motility patterns in the cell division of the diatom Seminavis robusta

**作者**: Jonas Ziebarth, Thomas Fuhrmann-Lieker
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-17

<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该研究通过细胞追踪和机器学习算法，探究了硅藻Seminavis robusta细胞分裂过程中子细胞大小差异是否影响分裂间隔时间或细胞运动性，发现分裂间隔时间无显著差异，与昼夜周期弱相关，且较小的子细胞运动性更高。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 许多硅藻在其营养生长阶段遵循尺寸缩减-尺寸恢复的循环，导致子代细胞在尺寸上存在差异。针对硅藻物种Seminavis robusta，我们通过多代细胞追踪技术，研究了这种尺寸差异是否同样反映在细胞分裂间期时长或细胞运动能力的差异上。本研究开发了一套基于机器学习的追踪检测系统与算法，结果显示：不同尺寸子代细胞的分裂间期时长无显著差异；其分裂周期与昼夜节律仅有微弱关联；且下壳面较小的子代细胞表现出更高的运动活性。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Many diatoms follow a size diminuation - size restoration cycle in their vegetative phase, leading to daughter cells that differ in size. For the diatom Seminavis robusta, we investigated by cell tracking over several generations whether the size difference reflects also in different intermitotic times or in the mobility of the cells. A tracking setup and machine-learning based detection algorithm was developed that revealed no significant difference in intermitotic times, a weak coupling to the day- night cycle, and a higher motility of the hypothecal, smaller daughter cell.

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: diatom, cell division, intermitotic time, cell motility, machine learning, cell tracking, Seminavis robusta, size diminution

### 279. ❌ Open Biomedical Knowledge Graphs at Scale: Construction, Federation, and AI Agent Access with Samyama Graph Database

**作者**: Madhulatha Mandarapu, Sandeep Kunkunuru
**期刊/来源**: arxiv
**发布日期**: 2026-03-16
**arXiv链接**: [http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15080v3](http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.15080v3)

**评分**: 0.0 / 29.0 ❌

**评分理由**: 论文研究的是生物医学知识图谱的构建、联邦查询和AI代理访问，具体涉及知识图谱数据库技术、ETL流程、数据集成和LLM工具访问。所有评分关键词均聚焦于医学影像分析、分割、深度学习诊断、预后预测、手术规划、多模态影像和基础模型等医学影像AI临床应用领域。论文内容完全不涉及医学影像处理、分析或基于影像的临床决策支持，因此所有关键词相关度均为0分。

</details>
<br>

!!! tip deepseek-chat TL;DR

    该论文解决了生物医学知识分散在多个孤立数据库中的问题，通过构建三个大规模开源生物医学知识图谱并实现跨图谱联邦查询和LLM代理访问，显著提升了生物医学问答的准确性和效率。

<details open>
<summary>摘要翻译</summary>

> 生物医学知识分散于孤立的数据库中——Reactome存储通路数据，STRING存储蛋白质相互作用，ClinicalTrials.gov存储研究注册信息，DrugBank存储药物词汇，DGIdb存储药物-基因相互作用，SIDER存储副作用信息。我们构建了三个开源生物医学知识图谱——通路知识图谱（整合5个来源，含118,686个节点与834,785条边）、临床试验知识图谱（整合5个来源，含7,774,446个节点与26,973,997条边）及药物相互作用知识图谱（整合3个来源，含32,726个节点与191,970条边）——这些图谱基于用Rust编写的高性能图数据库Samyama构建。
> 
> 我们的贡献包含三方面。首先，我们提出了一种可复现的ETL（提取-转换-加载）模式，用于从异构公共数据源构建大规模知识图谱，该模式具备跨源去重、批量加载（支持Python Cypher与Rust原生加载器）及便携式快照导出功能。其次，我们实现了跨知识图谱联邦查询：将三个快照加载至单一图租户后，可支持跨数据集的基于属性的关联查询。第三，我们引入了基于模式驱动的MCP（模型上下文协议）服务器生成技术，以支持大语言模型智能体访问，并在新的BiomedQA基准测试（40个药理学问题）中进行了评估：领域特定的MCP工具达到了98%的准确率，而模式感知的文本到Cypher查询为85%，独立GPT-4o模型为75%，且实现了零模式错误。
> 
> 所有数据源均为开放许可。整合后的联邦图谱（含790万个节点与2800万条边）在商用云硬件上加载仅需约3分钟，单知识图谱查询耗时80-100毫秒，跨知识图谱联邦关联查询耗时1-4秒。

</details>
<br>

<details>
<summary>摘要 (Abstract)</summary>

> Biomedical knowledge is fragmented across siloed databases -- Reactome for pathways, STRING for protein interactions, ClinicalTrials.gov for study registries, DrugBank for drug vocabularies, DGIdb for drug-gene interactions, SIDER for side effects. We present three open-source biomedical knowledge graphs -- Pathways KG (118,686 nodes, 834,785 edges from 5 sources), Clinical Trials KG (7,774,446 nodes, 26,973,997 edges from 5 sources), and Drug Interactions KG (32,726 nodes, 191,970 edges from 3 sources) -- built on Samyama, a high-performance graph database written in Rust.
>   Our contributions are threefold. First, we describe a reproducible ETL pattern for constructing large-scale KGs from heterogeneous public data sources, with cross-source deduplication, batch loading (Python Cypher and Rust native loaders), and portable snapshot export. Second, we demonstrate cross-KG federation: loading all three snapshots into a single graph tenant enables property-based joins across datasets. Third, we introduce schema-driven MCP server generation for LLM agent access, evaluated on a new BiomedQA benchmark (40 pharmacology questions): domain-specific MCP tools achieve 98% accuracy vs. 85% for schema-aware text-to-Cypher and 75% for standalone GPT-4o, with zero schema errors.
>   All data sources are open-license. The combined federated graph (7.9M nodes, 28M edges) loads in approximately 3 minutes on commodity cloud hardware, with single-KG queries completing in 80-100ms and cross-KG federation joins in 1-4s

</details>
<br>

**关键词**: biomedical knowledge graphs, graph database, data federation, ETL pipeline, LLM agents, MCP server, BiomedQA benchmark, open-source biomedical data
